Roman&quot;;">罗新平、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕耿松、吕国妹、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕先三</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、吕月霞、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拉珍（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村村妇，是扎陵湖乡河源新村南杰家族的女儿，已婚育有两个孩子，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>岁的女儿名叫塔嘎，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>岁的儿子名叫次嘉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">7</span>连<span lang="EN-US">28</span>号公民，哈萨克族穆斯林，清真寺伊玛目（政府指定的穆斯林领祷人），中国在押良心犯。自新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克族等少数族裔被中共新疆当局高压严控，采取集中教育培训（又称“再教育营”）以来，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年是被当局以各种罪由送“再教育营”，而后被再转拘捕、判刑最多的一年；腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔虽为中共官方指定的伊斯兰教伊玛目（领祷人），也从未参加任何宗教极端势力，但<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，却被察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团派出所警突然带走，并送某“再教育营”接受洗脑式培训（实则关押）；后因强行教育培训过程中不与官方妥协、合作，遂于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月之后，被察布查尔县警方刑拘和逮捕，指控其“念经（古兰经）即违法”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年下半年（具体日期不详），其案在犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县法院正式开庭审理受理，最终在无代理辩护律师及家人在场的情况下，被以“念古兰经”罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">23</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2041</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。目前在新疆生产建设兵团第七师奎屯监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/23.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/23.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兰立华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈阳市苏家屯区红菱镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年四十八岁。兰立华曾于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日依法控告江泽民遭报复抓捕，被苏家屯区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>个月，关押在辽宁女子监狱，被迫害致生命垂危；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日刑期满被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日她把一本台历送给一卖菜的老者，遭抓捕关押，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被沈阳市苏家屯区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兰太莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆市江北区法院对七十二岁的法轮功学员，女，家住重庆市合川区。曾遭看守所、洗脑班迫害　非法判刑一年缓两年。在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两天，各使用一张印有“法轮大法好 真善忍好”的纸币购物，并拥有法轮功真相资料，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日遭重庆江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">来桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。来桂芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">雷焕英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。雷焕英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">雷云波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，原荆州银行系统职工。因修炼法轮功被单位开除。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年在河南发真相资料被抓捕，后在武汉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。在范家台监狱被殴打，被超体力奴役。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年初，雷云波在云南被抓捕后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬，雷云波又被抓捕，至今仍被关押在荆州市沙市区看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">长春法轮功学员。冷凤翎女士目前被关押在吉林省女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日家人去监狱会见，才得知她被判处刑期<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被长春路园区国保、公安分局、长春和平大街派出所联合抓捕，并抄家，随后冷凤翎被刑事拘留，关押在第四看守所。现在冷凤翎被非法关押在吉林省女子监狱，构陷她的罪名是所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”，目前在第八监区第五支队，人员编号：<span lang="EN-US">70010194</span>。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">楞珠扎巴（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏歌手。楞珠扎巴于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被拘留，距离他<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月发行歌曲“黑帽子”不到两个月。在经过一年多的审前拘留之后，他于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑，被剥夺了辩护判权。楞珠扎巴最终判处<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年徒刑，理由是他在西藏那曲市比如县演唱批评政府镇压政策的歌曲。此前，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，楞珠扎巴与另一位著名的藏族歌手贡布丹增合唱一首名为《扎西央卓》的歌曲，其内容阐释境内藏人在中国政府的压制下遭受的状况和赞颂达赖喇嘛尊者，贡布丹增最终于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判处三年半徒刑。楞珠扎巴曾被监禁在那格监狱，目前他所监禁的位置和健康状况尚未清楚。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李佰华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨著名民主人士于云峰妻子。于云峰、李佰华夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭哈尔滨市公安局香坊分局以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。本次夫妇<span lang="EN-US">1</span>起被拘留具体事因未明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李碧云</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东佛山市顺德维权人士。李碧云曾参选顺德区人大代表、居委会主任，以往积极参与维权活动，经常上街举牌要求官员公开财产，多次被当局抓捕关押。以往她也曾因妨害公务罪入狱，在关押期间怀疑受到酷刑，导致两腿残障。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，李家姐弟三人因为洗手盆等废弃物品的事，被辖区新地派出所以涉嫌“盗窃罪”刑事拘传，在派出所呆了差不多<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个小时，<span lang="EN-US">26</span>号遭刑事拘留送去顺德区看守所。实际上，对李碧云姐弟的判决是当局对他们维权行动的报复。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广东维权人士李碧云、李彩云、李添强三姐弟涉嫌盗窃和妨害公务案宣判，李碧云两罪并罚获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月、李彩云和弟弟李添强以盗窃罪分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。李碧云刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李炳新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹的丈夫。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）被捕。数个月后，珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉。控方指魏小妹、李炳新及张涛涉嫌诈骗信徒奉献款，购买房产，构成诈骗罪。据知情人士披露，当局的指控缺乏有力证据，难以成立。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，香洲区民族宗教事务局取缔该教会，并扣留该教会近五十台电脑<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当局出动数十名公安，拘捕该教会十多名信徒，经过连续审讯及威胁，信徒被迫写下不利于教会领袖的证词。警方最终以诈骗罪刑事拘留该教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛。据知情人士披露，该案由珠海市政法委督办。当局先以“邪教罪”调查此案，但因查无实据，又改为“诈骗罪”问罪，这明显是一起宗教案件。广东珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）三人，被珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉至法院，指当事人诈骗奉献款，上述三人面临判刑。后无音信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林长春市农安县青山乡法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生。李聪女士<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在自家的油房被青山乡派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到农安县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李聪接到判决书，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚金两万元。李聪不服判决，上诉到长春市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，长春市中级法院未经开庭就宣布维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，李聪被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续关押迫害。入监后，每天晚上十二点睡、三点就被强制起来，坐小板凳。狱警纵容犯人虐待她，经常不给主食只给发糕、咸菜，逼强迫转化。在狱中，李聪一直遭受种种折磨：长时间罚站、饿刑、熬鹰、坐小凳、不准洗漱、围攻「洗脑」、人格侮辱等迫害外，还受到殴打，大冬天还开窗冻她，往她身上泼冷水。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李大红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副总经理。孙大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：李大红被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李大尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆州市监利县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十六岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午十一点左右，监利县国保大队、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、县公安局、特警出动大量警力，在同一时间合谋抓捕了李大尧、李乐成、朱春新、何成、王升贵五位法轮功学员，不由分说直接把人从家里带走，紧接着非法抄家，家中被翻得一片狼藉，电脑等大量私人物品被全部抢走，没留下什么清单。其中李大尧家的门被警察请来的撬锁人强行撬开。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后上诉，荆州中级法院维持原判。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被劫持到在湖北省范家台监狱关押。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李德宽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省蛟河市法河沿村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>，李德宽在蛟河市长安街的出租房内被街道派出所警察绑架，并遭非法抄家，其中有三套师父法像和很多大法书籍，家中九万五千余元现金也被警察拿走。五月一日下午，李德宽被押送到蛟河市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李德宽被吉林省蛟河市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李东军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林松原市前郭县红光农场九分场法轮功学员。李东军、黄秀华夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚七点多被松原市国保大队抓捕抄家。家里被抄走多部手机，两本《转法轮》、《洪吟五》一本，台历一个，对联一对，一个炼功播放器。后被关押在松原市善友看守所，最近得知他已经被庭审，李东军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现被关押在四平市公主岭监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李东哲（朝鲜）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，朝鲜族，辽阳市朝阳村基督教家庭教会负责人、牧师，良心犯。因中共当局加大了对民间意识形态、宗教信仰自由的打击力度，各地政府管理部门亦对基督教等不同宗教信仰群体及其聚会点采取了更激烈的打压逼迫，在此前提下，其所在教会尽管因加入“三自教会”已被官方认可，同时历时<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年，信徒达<span lang="EN-US">500</span>多人，但是仍被地方当局作为整治对象，遭到恶意打压与惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名教会负责者即骨干成员被辽阳市太子河区警方突然统一刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被辽阳市太子河区检察院以涉“非法经营罪”正式批捕，指控其身为教会负责人，自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，违反国家相关规定，唆使其教会骨干成员以“基督教朝光教会”名义购进、卖出海外非法宗教出版物<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万余本，涉及金额<span lang="EN-US">49</span>万多元，属于非法买卖行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院一审以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李凤祥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：李凤祥被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李钢：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。李钢老人<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月生，两年前，老人曾被绑架，被非法批捕，但因身体亮起红灯，被非法关押在看守所<span lang="EN-US">80</span>天后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚回家。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭绑架、构陷，大连市沙河口区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李广远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员天津市宁河区廉庄乡廉庄村人，与妻子莫伟秋于一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以来，夫妇俩多次被中共非法关押、劳教并被非法判刑，在被非法审判和监禁期间，夫妇俩多次遭到毒打和酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，李广远在孟庄集市向民众讲真相时，被廉庄乡派出所警察绑架，并遭非法抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日得知，天津市宁河区法院判处李广远<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李贵宝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京作家、网络写手。网名“肥猪满圈老李”。<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，李贵宝写了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>篇文章，<span lang="EN-US">7000</span>字，文中多为调侃，谈了疫情。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚上约<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点被警方带走，坐了多次笔录。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日去北京<span lang="EN-US">309</span>医院做了体检，办案中心做了核酸检测。夜送到看守所，因体温过高，看守所不收，遂取保候审。时间是<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日凌晨。然后移交到了检，去见了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，继续取保。取保期间做了两次补充侦查。再到了法院，去了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，续保。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，李贵宝因发文章被海淀法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被收押。这是一起典型的因言治罪的案件。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李桂华（黑龙江）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，佳木斯市木材厂退休工人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午三点多钟，李桂华在黑龙江省佳木斯市通江街与维新路交叉口处，李桂华给一名五十岁左右的男士讲法轮功真相时，遭报警，后被抓捕，被送到佳木斯市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李桂华被佳木斯市向阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李桂华不服上诉到佳木斯市中级法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，佳木斯市中级法院裁定维持向阳区法院对李桂华的一审原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李桂华（山东）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁左右。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，济南市铁路公安局、聊城市火车站派出所联合聊城市东昌府区国保大队、古楼派出所共十几个警察，闯入聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员华丽琴家中，把陈军、华丽琴、孙秀娥、李桂华、张亮、徐绍霞（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html#zip7"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李国爱</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。李国爱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李国庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。在电力公司电力调度室任职调度长。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被刑事拘留、关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李国庆刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李国欣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省平顶山市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。现年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。李国欣于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日上午在平顶山河滨公园，被平顶山市湛河区南环路派出所抓捕并抄家。平顶山市公安三分局批捕，当时被关押在舞钢看守所。被关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月，近悉已被鲁山县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，转到郑州监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李合珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北武汉市汉阳区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。李合珍老人独居。在中共对法轮功持续至今近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的迫害中，老人曾经因到北京上访被劫持到市第一拘留所、市第一看守所关押迫害四次，被非法关洗脑班一年多。李合珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在汉口中山公园，被宝丰路王家墩派出所警察抓捕，因由是“维稳”；警察把老人送到看守所非法关押，期间没有通知家人。又在不通知家人的情况下，公检法部门对老人秘密判刑四年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李红花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建漳州维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，李红花母亲庄金莲（<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）、女儿陈小玲（<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁）被漳州龙海市公安局刑事拘留。李红花（<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁）本人则在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被龙海法院以拒不履行法律文书义务的理由司法拘留十五日。后又被龙海公安刑事拘留。一家三代女性被控的罪名都是寻衅滋事，后均转为逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被指控的所谓犯罪的事实<span lang="EN-US">:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>起诉书指控李红花、庄金莲因对拆迁补偿不满，在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月间，多次到北京中南海周边非正常上访。并多次被训诫和处罚。其中李红花被训诫<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，庄金莲<span lang="EN-US">14</span>次，陈小玲<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次。李红花多年不停的维权，先后<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次被龙海市公安局行政拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月因参加福州一看门口放鞭炮迎接维权公民出狱，被刑拘一个月。福建漳州维权公民李红花一家三代女性被控寻衅滋事罪案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在漳州女子看守所内开庭审理，未当庭宣判。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在漳州女子看守所内第二次开庭宣判<span lang="EN-US">: </span>李红花获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、李红花母亲庄金莲获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、李红花女儿陈小玲则未被起诉。李红花刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆民营企业家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日李怀庆忽然被重庆警方以“涉黑”的名义抓捕，同时被抓捕的还有其妻子包艳以及其儿子并公司的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名员工（其中<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名员工均已离职）。随后，警察冻结了其公司和个人的近亿元资产。家属和律师收到的李怀庆的罪名先是“涉黑”，现在又改成“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，家属和律师原本已经收到了重庆市中级人民法院在这一天开庭审理李怀庆案件的通知，可诡异的是，家属和律师很快又收到一纸延期审理的通知书。这一延期，延到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月还音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在重庆开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，李怀庆被庆市第一中级法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法拘禁罪四项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。李怀庆是于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被警方以涉黑名义抓捕，其名下资产同时被全部冻结。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日家属收到重庆市南川监狱的信件，告知李怀庆已转到该监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潍坊护理职业学院<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁的大一学生 。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初李慧在校（益都校区）期间因选择不打疫苗，被学校老师校长或同学恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，老师带领警察闯入李慧宿舍，录像和搜查，搜出<span lang="EN-US">5</span>本大法书籍、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>百多张翻墙卡片和<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个护身符、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘。随后李慧被抓捕，后被构陷到检察院。李慧被关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月，家属一直被不允许会见，没有任何李慧的消息。后来家属得知，法院在<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>号对李慧进行庭审。后被青州市法院以所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李嘉惠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁，高新区人，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被重庆石桥铺高新区公安分局抓捕，被劳教两年，关押在重庆茅家山女子劳教所。。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。李嘉惠刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52185541"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李家周</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52185541;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：昆明法轮功学员。男。<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年生。云南宣威市龙场镇浓场村人，在昆明打工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、倪会仙由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。在抓捕杨靖波时，不法警察抓捕了在杨靖波家的法轮功学员李家周，并且进行抄家；又到李家周家里抢走了笔记本计算机、打印机及真相数据。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，西山区法院判处李家周<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李建新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠州市人，人称“惠州区伯”， 实名举报人。因长期网上实名举报广东惠州官员的贪腐行为，引起媒体关注和社会热议。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因其举报惠州市副市长黄锦辉，随遭遇报复性砍伤并被泼硫酸，导致其一只眼睛失明、手脚被砍断，留下终身残疾。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因其继续维权，坚持网络实名举报，被惠州市惠城区警方以涉“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被惠阳区检察院以涉“敲诈勒索”和“非法占用耕地”二罪批捕，并被羁押于惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被起诉于惠州市惠阳区法院，后其案又被因故移交到惠州市惠东县检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，河南太康县法轮功学员，本来是太康县回族小学教师。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功遭无端打压以后，因坚持信仰而屡遭迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，李杰和法轮功学员李慧平、谷玉荣、李艳华等人到乡下散发法轮功资料，被太康逊母口镇派出所抓捕，分别关押，李杰被关押在太康看守所，李慧平等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被关押在周口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李杰判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李晶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，李晶女士被长春市经开区分局与深圳街派出所警察抓捕并抢走她家的房门钥匙，警方后到出租屋抄家，抄走惠普高速打印机四台、激光打印机一台、电脑笔记本一台，真相电话十六部、大法书籍两套、大法真相资料等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在经开区法院被庭审，庭审没有通知李晶家属。目前李晶仍被非法关押在长春第四看守所，现在身体出现腹部疼痛，流血现象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日得知李晶被判刑十年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李军才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省新乡市原阳县基督教牧师。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">近年来，因反对中共当局强拆十字架，拒绝把教堂内“爱神爱人”标语改成“爱国爱教”及在教堂内建国旗台，随遭河南省当局打压逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被新乡市原阳县警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑事拘留，另有三名教会同工（即神职工作人员）亦被抓捕，随后几日，其所在中心堂十字架迅速被当地宗教局、公安局及城管等多个部门联合强拆，教堂内“爱神爱人”等标语被清除，教堂内被强行竖立起五星红旗；一个多月后，被抓三名同工均获取保候审，而其却被一直羁押不放，后被原阳县检察院正式批捕，指控其涉嫌“职务侵占、妨害公务和销毁账目”；截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件已在两度退回公安局补充侦查后，再次移送检察院，进入审查起诉阶段；据悉，其儿子称，当局对其父亲的一切指控均属莫须有罪名，旨在对其拒绝与官方合作态度进行刻意“打击报复”。在被关押长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个多月后，河南新乡原阳县家庭教会牧师李军才于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被以“职务侵占”、“妨害公务”及“销毁账目”三罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。另三人均判缓刑。目前被羁押于新乡市原阳县看守所（河南省新乡市原阳县葛埠口乡丘庙村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">453500</span>。）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李俊华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。李俊华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李柯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉籍，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日生，汉族，大学学历，被捕前无业。李柯于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日从武汉乘火车前往西宁，途中换上藏袍，于次日前往塔尔寺，在下午<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点<span lang="EN-US">04</span>分购票进入寺院。并且在塔尔寺不同的地方展示标语和雪山狮子旗和<span lang="EN-US">FREE TIBET(</span>自由西藏<span lang="EN-US">)</span>标语，，让路过游客帮忙拍照。随后被塔尔寺驻寺警察拘留，随后于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被正式批捕。该案于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在西宁市中级人民法院审理，李柯被控煽动分裂国家罪，当庭没有宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。随后李国庆、女儿李蕾被关押在芦台派出所；妻子于波被刑拘。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李蕾刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李霖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆乌鲁木齐公民李霖因言获罪<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被新疆警方刑事拘留。原因是其曾在海外的推特上发推批评新疆当局的政策，新疆警方先是以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”对其逮捕，后李霖遭控“煽动颠覆国家政权”，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李玲莲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东省梅州市梅城法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，家住广东梅州城区江南团结路，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被抓捕、抄家，后被关押在梅江区（芹洋）看守所。后李玲莲一审被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚款三万五千元。后上诉，二审维持原判，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劫持到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李龙全：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，贵州省毕节市纳雍县人，又名李老五，中国在押维权人士。因长期未得到政府赔付的足额退耕还林补偿，索要遭拒，故而多次上访；曾因揭露当地政府为征地进行暗箱操作，不仅拒付村民合理补偿而且还打残村民，其本人亦遭殴打，肠子被打漏；其被迫无奈走上漫长艰难的维权之路；然上访几年，倾家荡产而无果；曾因和多个维权访民到当地王家寨政府及县政府门口拉横幅上访投诉，使得地方执政者十分不满；省委第九巡视组进驻纳雍县时，曾因到巡视组住地要求与巡视组人员见面，表达合理诉求，不得见，便拉幅喊冤，抗议政府强征、暴力执法及三条命案，遂遭到地方当局的严厉打压和疯狂报复；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其和<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名维权访民一同欲赴京上访，反映全村<span lang="EN-US">970</span>亩退耕还林土地款被县政府非法扣留事宜，不料被访民中的政府内线告发，其一行<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余人在贵州省水城黄土坡“新雨旅社”集合时，被赶来的纳雍县警方随即抓捕，其中除有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多人跑掉之外，剩下<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被悉数拘留，后虽放出<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，但其却被一直被刑拘于纳雍县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被纳雍县检察院以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，控其因组织村民在当地政府门口，用拉横幅、喊口号及游行等方式表达诉求，并将抗议过程拍摄、发布到“六四天网”，因此触犯了有关法律，属于违法行为；据悉，其儿子曾去派出所询问父亲为何被捕，竟遭警方殴打并被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年某日，被贵州省纳雍县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，经贵州省毕节市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。目前疑在贵州省都匀监狱（贵州省黔南布依族苗族自治州都匀市羊场街<span lang="EN-US">26</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">558000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李美莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员。自一九九九年七月，法轮功遭受江氏中共集团镇压以来，李美莲为坚持自己的信仰，告诉世人法轮功被迫害的真相，曾遭两次劳教（共计约三年多）、一次判刑（五年）。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李美莲再次被抓捕，李美莲在江西省女子监狱脚筋被割断致残，丈夫离世，家中的儿子无人照看，生意兴旺的店铺无人料理关闭，父母双亲中有一个永远地离开了她。目前获悉其已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李美青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">北京维权人士。李美青家在北京市丰台区石榴庄，因自家房屋遭到强拆，多次上访无果，还遭到当地政府的严酷打压，她的妹妹李焕君因此流亡美国。李焕君曾经多次阻拦习近平、李克强等中国领导人访美车队喊冤。然而，不仅维权毫无进展，甚至被安保打伤。李焕君的女儿、母亲亦遭到株连，被当局以“可能危害国家安全”限制出境。据李美青妹妹李焕君通报：她姐姐、北京维权人士李美青<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初在北京被政府和公安以“两会期间维稳”的名义控制多日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午李美青被当局维稳人员逼服下上百片安眠药。送医急救后遭刑事拘留。现羁押于北京丰台看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李美荣<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">东菏泽市单县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬，黄坤益、李美荣夫妇去单县黄冈镇发放法轮功小册子时被镇派出所警察抓捕。李美荣老人被送到菏泽市女子看守所关押，黄坤益老人因高血压被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被通过视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，李美荣老人<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，黄坤益老人<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，李美荣老人从看守所被送到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E8%8F%8F%E6%B3%BD%E5%B8%82%E5%8D%95%E5%8E%BF%E9%BB%84%E5%9D%A4%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E7%BE%8E%E8%8D%A3%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430285.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E8%8F%8F%E6%B3%BD%E5%B8%82%E5%8D%95%E5%8E%BF%E9%BB%84%E5%9D%A4%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E7%BE%8E%E8%8D%A3%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430285.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李敏舫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，宝鸡消防厂退休职工，家住宝鸡市金台区宝平路。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日以取保候审的方式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，宝鸡市金台区检察院通知李敏舫已被转为监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李明书：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州省桐梓县燎原镇花园村年近古稀的村民李明书，因与其他村民举报原镇长王国燕、村支书令狐昌华、杨小勇、国土所长易正芳在征地拆迁中，徇私枉法、以权谋私、中饱私囊，侵犯村民的利益，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在贵阳机场被抓捕，在被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后被正式逮捕。李明书在看守所换仓后受到牢头狱霸的威胁，要其赶快认罪，不然，就要拳头伺候。家人要求给父亲送冬天的帽子不被允许。后案件信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李明哲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，祖籍安徽省人，实为中华民国台北市人，前台湾立委许钟碧霞国会办公室助理，前台北市议员谢明达竞选总部助选员，台湾民主进步党党员，非政府组织“人权公约施行监督联盟”<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>志工，首个被中国大陆公审的台湾人，人权活动者。早期曾参加台湾新党青年军，并在大学期间因受自由思潮启蒙，与现任妻子李净瑜共同参与反对台湾高学费运动。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年曾先后任台湾民主进步党社会发展部专员和前新台湾文化基金会专员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月曾担任非政府组织“人权公约施行监督联盟”志工。多年来，曾因长期关注中国人权状况及民主维权运动等议题，尤其是基于大陆许多人有阅读人权、近代史、政党选举等书籍的需要，自费邮赠大量文学与社科类书籍，而一直受到中共当局的严密监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月曾因邮寄台湾书籍而遭到中共当局的查扣没收。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日当其前往中国大陆，途径澳门关卡再转入境到珠海拱北口岸时，被莫名消失，其妻及社会各界频繁呼吁亦无消息，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才从中国官方获悉，其被国家安全部以涉“危害国家安全”罪由拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被湖南省检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，被控其“自<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来，频繁进入大陆活动，与大陆有关人员勾结，制定行动纲领，建立非法组织，策划、实施颠覆我国家政权的活动”，属违法犯罪行为。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其案在岳阳市中级法院开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前被羁押于湖南省岳阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李其文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东临清市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日左右被临清国保抓捕，被非关押于临清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日李其文被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李谦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住昆明市西山区白马干休所。因坚持修炼法轮功，李谦女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早上，因疑似派出所警察对她进行跟踪和监控，李谦只身来到昆明市棕树营派出所反映情况，并讲述法轮功被迫害真相，警察在送她出来的时候，李谦给了她几份法轮功真相资料，并嘱咐她退出邪党（党、团、队）组织才能保平安。结果被派出所警察抓捕抄家。关押在昆明市看守所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日李谦即被昆明市西山区公安分局逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被昆明市西山区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金一万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被送到云南省第二女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李翘楚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生，女权主义者，劳工问题研究者。大学本科毕业于中国人民大学劳动人事学院，研究生毕业于英国约克大学并获公共政策硕士学位，其后于清华大学从事研究助理的工作。李翘楚长期参与、关注和研究中国大陆的劳工、女权和民间维权议题。她的研究领域涉及劳工视角的养老保险等政策问题。此外，她还积极参加各种民间自发行动，比如声援北京郊区“清理低端人口”事件中的农民工、反<span lang="EN-US">996</span>、<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>、武汉疫情下的性别暴力问题等。<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>公民案发生后，当局大规模搜捕参与厦门聚会的公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，李翘楚在她的男友许志永流亡期间被北京警方传唤<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时，她之后在网络发表《戴手铐跨新年：<span lang="EN-US">12</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">∙</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被传唤经过》，由此开始实名发声，声援<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>案。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李翘楚被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被指定居所监视居住<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个。她根据自己被秘密关押的经历写下了《李翘楚：被连坐煽颠、指定监视居住的<span lang="EN-US">120</span>天》系列文章，详细讲述了自己被关押期间所遭受的酷刑及不人道虐待。当李翘楚了解到许志永在指监期间遭受酷刑后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日就伙食问题向临沂市公安局寄出了政府信息公开申请，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日就伙食远低于国家标准和高价买餐的问题对临沭县看守所进行了控告，就驻看守所检察官的不履行监督职责进行了投诉，并对临沂市公安局局长和临沂县看守所所长的违法行为进行控告。<span lang="EN-US"> 2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李翘楚被山东警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”押往临沂，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李翘楚案被退回临沂市公安局补充侦查，期限一个月。而此前李翘楚家属申请的取保候审被驳回。目前李翘楚被关押在临沂市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/910.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/910.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李瑞玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市朝阳区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，李瑞玲粘贴大法资料，被东城区花市派出所警察跟踪、抓捕。随后七八个警察带着李瑞玲到家里抄家，抄走了大法书籍、电脑、真相资料等私人物品。李瑞玲<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被非法开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉，李瑞玲被东城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李绍志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十四岁，原为佳木斯市煤矿机械厂工人。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日去北京为法轮功上访被抓捕，后劳教一年。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日李绍志和其他十一名法轮功学员不堪忍受劳教所的虐待，逃离劳教所，从此被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，李绍志回到家乡佳木斯，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被举报抓捕，后被判刑五年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出狱。之后去了哈尔滨，在哈尔滨多年来靠打工维持生活。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，租住在哈尔滨南岗区的李绍志，被长春市南关区民康派出所警察，协同哈尔滨市警察在他租住的楼前抓捕。被关押在长春市第三看守所。长春市南关区法院<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日对法轮功学员李绍志开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李树南：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖北省荆州市监利县白螺镇人，监利县白螺镇五里庙村村民，司法不公举报人，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，曾因承包邻村彭阮村<span lang="EN-US">110</span>亩土地搞多种养殖期间，当地监利县柘木乡政府官员非法平整土地致其岳母家农田出现严重损毁现象，其协助家人被迫向上反映，以求妥善解决问题，孰料多次投诉无果，反起冲突、被造假；后其逐渐认识到投诉无门，上访反被造假诬告皆因地方官员相互勾结贪污公款（即：以县委书记为首勾结乡村干部做假帐截留救灾资金，倒卖救灾物资，贪污工程青苗补偿款），坑害百姓所致，至此开始逐级上访；曾因其举报维权触动了地方官员的私利（即采用重复申报水利工程项目等诈骗国家资金），而遭当局强力逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其曾遭报复性殴打，致其身体终生残疾；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因其夫妻二人承包的鱼塘在地方干部的纵容下被人破坏，承包合同被单方废止，而使其直接经济损失多达<span lang="EN-US">60</span>余万元；曾因其妻陈呈香出于义愤，采取极端抗议方式点火自焚，以求正义公道，其为此提起上诉，但在同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日信访投诉听证会上却因地方当局提供伪证，其夫妇二人被警方分别行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因其妻两次进京投诉而被监利县警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共秩序罪”刑拘，后又被宣布劳动教养，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日才被释放，故而其维权抗争之心日益弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在京信访反映冤情时遭到北京警方地毯式抓铺，后被移交给监利县截访人员遣返原籍，又被关进某宾馆式黑监狱，遭到群殴，致其身体多处受伤；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被荆州市监利县警方从家中突然带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，知其早已被转正式批捕，其案现已被检察院以同罪由移交至湖北省荆州市监利县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，湖北省荆州市监利县访民李树南、陈呈香夫妻二人寻衅滋事案，在监利县检察院视频开庭，被告人大女儿李艳华，律师尚满庆、杨高华到达现场。在庭审过程中，检察官以其夫妻二人多次扰乱公共秩序、敲诈勒索予以定罪，建议给予<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年刑期。未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，李树南、陈呈香夫妇分别获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。目前二人均被羁押于荆州市监利县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李淑萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，家住沈阳市皇姑区<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台子地区。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，李淑萍在北京遭抓捕，被劳教两年，关押到北京女子劳教所奴役。李淑萍<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沈阳市和平区国保大队便衣警察跨区抓捕，被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被沈阳市和平区法院在网络上庭审。近日获悉，李淑萍已被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李淑云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，北京市丰台区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被北京市永定门外派出所警察抓捕，关押在北京市东城区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李伟涛：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，辽阳法轮功学员李伟涛、王永生、国世游、谷林杰、汤显贺、罗丽被辽阳市白塔公安分局国保警察马文博等人绑架、抄家，当时国世游身体不适被多个警察抬着抓走的。辽宁省辽阳市白塔区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李伟涛等六名法轮功学员判刑，刑期是：李伟涛<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。李伟涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李文波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">昆明法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，，昆明市晋宁县昆阳街道办事处古城村人。中共迫害法轮功的二十多年中，李文波因为坚持信仰法轮功，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年入冤狱<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，因所在的月山小区居委会展出污蔑法轮大法及其创始人的展板，李文波致信给晋宁区公、检、法工作人员、月山小区工作人员，澄清事实，并要求撤销展板。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，古城二组因他修炼法轮功，而被村委会扣发一万块钱。李文波针对此事，写信给村委会领导，指出此种做法不合理，要求退还扣发的钱。李文波依法将两封信递交给负责的相关部门及人员，希望所反映的问题得到解决。这本是作为一个公民的合法信访行为，但却于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，接到昆阳派出所打来的电话，叫他第二天去派出所核对一个案子。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日当晚李文波被拘捕，被扣押到昆明市晋宁县看守所。这次李文波在看守所被关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月后，又因消化道出血、空腔脏器穿孔、肠梗阻、重度贫血等严重疾病，不适合继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李文波以取保候审形式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，西山区法院对“取保候审”在外的李文波开庭审理，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上旬，李文波接到了昆明市西山区法院对他判刑五年，并处罚金一万元，还要销毁从他家中搜走的私人书籍及材料。李文波当即表示要上诉。未收监。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，李文波在公共汽车站炼功，被人恶意举报后遭警察抓捕抄家。后李文波被关押在晋宁县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，昆明市西山区法院又对李文波开庭。之后，李文波家属接到了西山区法院的判决，李文波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年（加上之前正在上诉被判的五年）。李文波不服判决，向昆明市中级法院上诉，但中院依然维持了原判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李文波被关押到云南省第一监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李文德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，商丘市民权县双塔乡韭菜里村农民，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日曾因信仰、维护法轮功而被河南省地方当局处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。获释后，因坚持信仰自由并继续宣传法轮功真相，而于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年又被地方当局以涉邪教罪名义处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，关押于河南省许昌市劳教所；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年秋，曾因与多人一起去商丘市民权县野鸡岗乡宣传法轮功，而被民权县警方刑拘、逮捕，后被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被关押于河南省新密市新密监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年出狱后，因控诉前中共国家领导人江泽民打压迫害法轮功成员，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被商丘民权县警方再次以涉“邪教罪”刑拘，关押于河南省睢县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月在不通知其家人的情况下被秘判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。据悉，因其多次被非法关押，其<span lang="EN-US">84</span>岁老母受到多次惊吓，已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份去世。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李晓波：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省人，前四川省仁寿县副书记、前四川省蒲江县县长，原某房产公司总经理，法轮功修炼者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年中共将法轮功定为“邪教”之后，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年遂被四川省成都市警方逮捕，并被当地法院以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，关押于四川省德阳监狱，受尽摧残折磨，直至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年才准予获释；出狱后，其信仰意志弥坚，继续进行法轮功修炼并传播法轮功真相，遂遭致当局的严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因其在成都市龙泉驿区金堂县给村民散发法轮功真相传单，被当地洪安派出所警方强行抓走（注：当时被野蛮抓捕的还有其子李喆，后因李喆已是加拿大籍公民，遂被当局强行遣回加拿大）并被刑拘，其家被抄，且所有被抄物品包括四台计算机和打印机等，均不给开据任何没收清单；后被正式逮捕，超期关押于四川省成都市龙泉驿看守所；<span
