lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终被四川省成都市龙泉驿法院再次以“利用邪教组织颠覆国家法律罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。目前在四川省德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李新德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，从<span lang="EN-US">80</span>年代从事业余新闻报道工作，到<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代末从事专业新闻报道工作。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日创办中国舆论监督网，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发布《下跪的副市长——山东济宁市副市长李信丑行录》，<span lang="EN-US">46</span>天后，李信被逮捕，最终被判无期徒刑。李新德成为新闻界的新闻人物，被誉为中国民间舆论监督第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人。李新德利用网络反腐维权的事迹，许多媒体均与报道。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，江苏省邳州市公安局以李新德涉嫌“经营罪”指定居所监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月后的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日转为刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日经邳州市检察院批准逮捕。现羁押在邳州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，江苏省邳州市法院以“经营罪”判处“中国舆论监督网”创办人李新德有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李新德刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李行军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员，荆州市实验中学的老师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多钟，李行军从母亲家出来，刚下楼，就被国保、西门派出所警察、学校保卫科等多人抓捕，他们对他拳打脚踢，打的满脸是血。被强行带上警车后，就送到西门看守所去了。妻子孙江怡也被抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日才开庭。李行军、孙江怡夫妇被庭审，两人都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李雪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东胶州法轮功学员。一家人因信仰被迫害多年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李雪及其母亲宋桂香通过快递分别向北京最高检察院、最高法院邮寄了刑事控告书，控告江泽民发起对法轮功学员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，以阜安派出所负责人想找她们母女“谈话”的名义将宋桂香、李雪骗至派出所，然后羁押于青岛普东看守所进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李雪被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年重刑，现在山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李彦春：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河北省秦皇岛市人，原多家医院管理工作者、院长，医学专家，学科带头人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾从事医学专业<span lang="EN-US">40</span>多年，拥有丰富的医院管理经验；退休前，曾在当地多家医院从事管理工作并担任过院长；曾发表过<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余篇医学科技论文并担任本学科带头人；然而，虽其（含其妻子裴玉贤）职业生涯及其敬业、努力给社会与民众带来了可喜的贡献，但却因信仰法轮功而遭致中共当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其夫妇二人到秦皇岛市卢龙县散发法轮功宣传挂历，被恶人告发，随被卢龙县双望派出所警方抓捕，且被戴手铐、脚镣等，审讯时，惨遭殴打和刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其夫妇二人涉邪教案被卢龙县警方递交到卢龙县检察院，后被卢龙县检察院以涉嫌邪教罪予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其案在秦皇岛市昌黎县法院开庭受理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被河北省秦皇岛市昌黎县法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，后因身体极差原因被准予保外就医；其妻裴玉贤亦被以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；二人不服判决，当庭均表示上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其被秦皇岛市卢龙县双望派出所警方再次收监逮捕，旋即被送往监狱接续服刑；其妻裴玉贤亦在此前被送河北省石家庄女子监狱服刑。目前在河北省冀东监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李艳杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，李艳杰被大庆市局伙同让胡路岗龙分局警察抓捕并抄家，说是李艳杰在让胡路明湖花园小区发放法轮功资料。李艳杰自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被抓捕后一直被关押在大庆市第二看守所，家人探视权被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，家人委托律师到看守所看望李艳杰，才知道李艳杰被大庆市让葫路区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李艳秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州市太和区，法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十二岁。她修炼法轮功十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李艳秋在向世人发送法轮功台历时，遭锦州太和区国保大队警察绑架，李艳秋家中的电脑、大法书籍等私人物品，被警察强行拿走。后她被关押到锦州市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午，锦州市太和区法院在不通知家属的情况下，在锦州看守所对李艳秋秘密开庭，法院指定了法律援助律师为她作有罪辩护，而李艳秋一直没有认过罪。法官在李艳秋身体极度虚弱、不能独立行走、不能完整表达意愿的情况下，匆匆走了过场。后获知李艳秋已经被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李燕群：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，广东省佛山市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，李燕群曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在广东省女子监狱被虐待迫害的身体不能自理，手脚都严重变形了，至今还未完全康复。因行动不便，老人很少出门。李燕群女士一个人居住，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，在家中被中共抓捕和抄家，一直被非法关押在佛山市第三人民医院（精神病医院）。当局以防疫为由，拒绝家属和辩护律师会见。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，李燕群被佛山市禅城区法院视频庭审。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师被告知李燕群被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚金七千元，目前，家人仍然不知李燕群被非法关押在哪里。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李一恒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市大兴区亦庄法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，北京市大兴区法轮功学员李一恒被大兴区公安分局亦庄派出所两个便衣警察抓捕，关押于北京市大兴区看守所。后获悉，李一恒被北京市大兴区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李银秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人梁子亮的妻子，梁子亮和李银秀<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省沈阳市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，准备乘火车去外地看望生病的父亲，在沈阳火车站安检时，被查出携带有法轮功的物品，后被沈阳火车站派出所警察孙斌等人抓捕，搜出大法书<span lang="EN-US">1</span>本，法轮功真相粘贴、真相币、护身符、播放器等。随后，她被关押到沈阳市看守所数月。在没有通知家属的情况下，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，李玉娥被沈阳市于洪区法院远程开庭，一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李玉娥不服一审判决，随上诉至沈阳市中级法院。中级法院二审于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，刑期改判为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李玉凤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，河南省焦作市人，基督徒，维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末，曾因家中惨遭两次政府不当拆迁，损失巨大，其被迫提起诉讼，打赢了官司，但因被告是当地政府，法院不予执行，故而其被迫上访维权；曾因不断维权，被当局进行恶意打击报复，并以“妨害公务罪”对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后其继续状告地方政府，再遭逼迫，又被劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；两次入狱，备受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因与他人前往监狱迎接“新公民运动”维权代表袁冬出狱，并率先打出横幅“欢迎袁冬从小监狱回到大监狱”，又被北京大兴区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被北京市大兴区检察院批捕，至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被取保候审释放。关押期间，曾被突击审讯（且大多是疲劳审讯）达<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次，身心惨遭迫害。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又因在北京南站照相，被北京市丰台公安刑拘一个月后，又被焦作市当局带回原籍补充侦查再次刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被河南省焦作市中站区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。其不服，提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日经焦作市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。获释后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，李玉凤在北京申诉又遭绑架押回，后被刑事拘留，直接送往焦作看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被焦作市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其案已被地方检察院起诉至焦作市中站区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日开庭宣判，李玉凤获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前被羁押于河南省焦作市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4_30.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4_30.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李昱函：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">岁，现北京执业律师，<span lang="EN-US">709</span>王宇案的代理律师。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年考取律师资格，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年开始在辽宁执业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年为逃避公安迫害从辽宁逃到北京，目前于北京市敦信律师事务个人所执业。李昱函患有心脏疾病，并曾多次受到公安的酷刑对待。李昱函律师最后一次和外界接触是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。当天，她向弟弟发短信，说自己被沈阳市公安局和平分局警察带走。之后便下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午，李昱函的家属对外透露，李律师现已被沈阳市公安局和平分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被正式批捕。律师已获会见。获知李昱函患有房颤心律失常、冠心病、甲亢、弥漫性胃炎等病，她包里的诊断证明都有，抓捕他在派出所里，她就感觉这次就活不成了。此案被当局故意拖延了近<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的时间，不审不判。目前李昱函羁押在沈阳市第一看守所。沈阳市和平区法院定于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日开庭审理，但开庭当日却取消了开庭。根据该法院报请最高人民法院人民法院批准，本案一次次延期。案件最近一次再次被延期到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。李昱函会见律师说：“法官让我认罪认罚，我说我没有罪，怎么认呢？法官说检察院的量刑建议是<span lang="EN-US">5</span>～<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李源东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省茂名市法轮功学员、广东化州人，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，大学毕业后进入广东省茂名港务监督局工作。李源东<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮功，但两个月后，中共开始了对法轮功的疯狂镇压，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年给信访局写信、并<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次去北京为法轮功上访，茂名市公安局因此两次对李源东劳教各<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，遭酷刑虐待，妻离子散。为求生计，到广州打工，又给民众讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，结果被恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2019</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日</span>被广州市海珠区公安分局沙园派出所警察刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被海珠区检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被构陷到海珠区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被构陷到海珠区法院。关押在广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，李源东被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。李源东当庭表示要上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%8E%9F%E8%8C%82%E5%90%8D%E6%B8%AF%E7%9B%91%E5%B1%80%E5%85%AC%E5%8A%A1%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E6%BA%90%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-430337.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%8E%9F%E8%8C%82%E5%90%8D%E6%B8%AF%E7%9B%91%E5%B1%80%E5%85%AC%E5%8A%A1%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E6%BA%90%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-430337.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李展：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">深圳佳士案维权工人。“<span lang="EN-US">7.27</span>大抓捕”第<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，余浚聪、米久平、刘鹏华、李展四人被正式逮捕。被抓捕已经两年，仍未开庭判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李占金</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。北京大学退休高级工程师、法轮功学员。一九九六年开始修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，李占金多次遭中共迫害，被非法拘留、强制“洗脑”，被非法劳教、非法判刑。李占金于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午被北京市海淀区公安分局、燕园派出所张艳辉等七个警察闯入家中抓捕、抄家。后李占金老人一直被非法关押在海淀区看守所。被绑架关押构陷近两年，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被海淀法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李振洋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省朝阳市法轮功学员。李振洋是朝阳市一个普通人，是靠蹬板车或做苦力活维持生计。李振洋自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被抓捕后，一直被非法关押在朝阳市看守所。李振洋于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李忠秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省广水市维权人士，女。李忠秀位于广水市中心东正商业街<span lang="EN-US">19</span>号房屋，共计平房<span lang="EN-US">4</span>间，占地面积<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多平米。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，广水市政府对东正街实施改造，按照改造的政策，李忠秀可以在原址上按政府统一规划重建。然而，当广水市政府与广水市广房房地产公司以欺诈手段，及房屋拆迁行政部门枉法裁决将李忠秀房屋拆除后，却将李忠秀回建的地皮低价出卖给了有官方背景的人，导致李忠秀无法重建，遂被迫上访。李忠秀是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在北京遭到截访的，广水市公安局对其刑事拘留，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，该案在广水市法院开庭审理，李忠秀为自己做了无罪辩护，而公诉机关建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，按照刑事诉讼法的程序规定，现在李忠秀已处于被超期羁押中，估计当局会判刑建议量刑的上限。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">利瓦伊棕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省济南法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。家住济南市章丘区普集镇麻秸村，他在邻近的滨州市邹平区临池镇一家耐火砖厂打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，利瓦伊棕打工下班后，在临池镇发法轮功材料，被临池派出所警察通过摄像监控发现。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日清晨，利瓦伊棕正在耐火砖厂干活时，遭到临池派出所警察抓捕，随后，利瓦伊棕被关押在邹平区看守所至今。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被山东滨州市邹平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，家人才得知此消息。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎金凤<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省云浮市法轮功学员。黎金凤于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被云安区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份上诉维持原判，将在广州女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432491.html#211012222131-2"><span style="color: windowtext;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432491.html#211012222131-2</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁春华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林市龙潭区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在吉林市大华市场与商家兑换真相币时，被警察跟踪绑架，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元左右真相币被警察抢走，梁春华先被行政拘留十天。三月二十七日拘留到期，警察直接将梁春华拉走，抄家，抢走工资卡、存折等物品，家里被劫的空荡荡。然后将梁春华又劫持到吉林市看守所关押，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被关押在吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁顺景<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，广东省梅州市梅县区城东镇人，原中国工商银行梅州分行职工，梅州城区江南团结路苏泊尔电器店负责人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因为人谦和、厚道而深受他人好评；又因其与其妻邓秀芬在当地共同承办苏泊尔电器店（主营电器厨器专卖批发），生意上注重诚实守信，随其公司至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底时已有较大发展；但因梁顺景、邓秀芬夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在信仰追求上笃信并积极宣传法轮功，随遭广东省梅州市当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在开车外出讲解宣传法轮功时，被事先蹲坑等候的梅州市梅江区警方及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室人员联合抓走，其家遭查抄，当场搜走法轮功书籍多套、计算机、打印机及银行卡、身份证等个人对象（如）多件，并将其日用汽车也拉走扣留；次日，其妻因血压高达<span lang="EN-US">180/230</span>，让家人暂时接回，其本人则被梅江区警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，关押至梅江区芹黄看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被梅江区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在梅州市梅江区法院开庭审理；虽因该法院违反法定诉讼程序，其辩护律师曾据理要求法院重新开庭审判，但其与其妻仍然被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判；其中<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">，梁顺景被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，其妻邓秀芬被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并各处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，经广东省梅州市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其妻邓秀芬刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所时被查出身体长有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个肿瘤，在被庭审时其辩护权及辩护律师执业权被剥夺；其承办的苏泊尔电器店因长时无人经营，故被迫关门。目前在广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱（广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘镇<span lang="EN-US">/</span>广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">梁琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</b>其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁香姣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，湖北省武汉市蔡甸区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，梁香姣被汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到武汉女子监狱，遭酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，梁香姣被几个便衣警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留。被羁押在武汉市第一看守所。经过一年多的构陷，据悉武汉市汉阳区法院将于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日晚上六点庭审梁香姣。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午两点半，在武汉市汉阳区法院庭审据悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市丰台区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，梁新在北京东城区亮果厂胡同发法轮功资料时，被监控器监控；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，梁新被东城区石景山派出所抓捕、抄家，许多私人物品被抢劫。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，梁新被北京东城区公安分局非法拘留。关押在北京市东城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁展鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东深圳市福田区法轮功学员，女士，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，梁展鸿老人在家中被抓捕，所谓的原因是她给小区保安讲法轮功被举报。遭受绑架几个月后，梁展鸿老人从福田看守所转入南山看守所，目前已经被非法关押在南山看守所将近一年。后得知已遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，未上诉。目前已收到通知，将被送广州女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁子亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人，梁子亮与妻子李银秀，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖光慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川绵阳市涪城区新华厂家属区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日下午，廖光慧，被十几个身穿便衣的彪形大汉（后了解是花园派出所警察）突然闯入家中，未出示任何搜捕证和身份证明等，就强行控制家人自由行动，像土匪一样抄家近三个小时之久，强行抢走私人物品：笔记本计算机</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">台，手机、打印机、刻录机、现金几百元，大法书籍、大法师父法像等个人物品。廖光慧被关押在绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日被绵阳市涪城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金三千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廖杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、大连市庄河市法轮功学员。廖杰于<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，家居庄河市长岭镇。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，她在蓉花山镇双烈寺集讲真相被蓉花山镇派出所警察抓捕。当日下午，警察上门抄家，抢劫了一些私人物品。廖杰被关押在姚家看守所，后被构陷到庄河市法院，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廖元华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，原武穴市农业局纪委书记，因讲述法轮功真相，曾被判刑三年，现在被非法关押在武穴市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。程学珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林海英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。李瑞华林海英母女<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在家中被官渡公安警察分别处以形式拘留和取保候审。据<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华区检察院的指控，李瑞华<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，在昆明市官渡区人民东路向过往群众散发 “为你而来”光盘并宣扬法轮功时被昆明市公安局官渡分局金马派出所协警抓捕、抢劫法轮功光盘<span lang="EN-US">5</span>片，公安警察赶到现场后将抓捕，后搜查李瑞华和林海英共同居住的房间，当场抓捕了林海英，同时抢劫了大量法轮功真相资料及光盘，不法警察搜查过程中，林海英多次制止警察犯法，朝窗户向小区高呼“法轮大法好”等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，李瑞华和林海英母女被五华法院开庭；林海英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千，李瑞华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：林海英<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林丽卿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月十<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，林丽卿到揭阳市榕城区法轮功学员林玩贞家读《转法轮》，被前来骚扰的榕城区国保大队伙同揭阳市榕华派出所警察抓捕。当时，在林玩贞家读《转法轮》的还有法轮功学员吴荣端。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨，林玩贞、吴荣端被释放。林丽卿则一直被关押于揭阳市看守所。林玩贞由于被惊吓过度，被释放一个多月后去世。后得知她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林茂成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连市金州区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，林茂成给陌生人讲法轮功，被他诬告后遭抓捕抄家，非法拿走大法书籍、计算机、打印机、身份证、驾驶证等物品。林茂成被劫持到派出所期间强制照相，录指纹、声音、验血、做完笔录后，逼他签字未果。半夜后，人被放回，监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，林茂成被大连普兰店检察院批捕，并被大连大孤山边防派出所强制关押在大连开发区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，林茂成被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：辽宁省沈阳市著名维权人士林明洁的哥哥。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与弟弟林明洁一起遭抓捕，后被被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见林明洁是才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">是辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林燕梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林在务：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，化名林大海、林忠，福建省福清市人，福清市东瀚镇东瀚村田尾<span lang="EN-US">17</span>号村民，职业不详，“耶和华见证人”信徒、传道人，新疆耶和华见证人教会正规先驱（类似于基督教的长老），中国在押良心犯。因信仰耶和华见证人教派，并被委任在新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒地区做正规先驱（即该教会一种重要职务），在库尔勒市组成家庭聚会，举行上百次大型聚会及成员培训，大力发展信徒，随遭极左思维极强的中共当局严打狠批；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在“耶和华见证人案”大抓捕中，被库尔勒市警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”与多人悉数抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，并被指控称，其因打着基督教旗号，组织教会聚会， “宣扬所谓政治中立，煽动成员及他人不履行公民法定义务”，破坏了国家的法律法规，所以属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人涉邪教案被警方向当地检察院提起公诉；后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被检察院发回补侦，但同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又已被补查重报；至今待审未判，且无更多具体信息；据悉，曾在看守所内因拒绝唱“红歌”等，常遭连体铐、抱铐等体罚虐待。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘爱华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省辽阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，辽阳市警察跟踪刘爱华。刘爱华被抓捕、抄家，关押在辽阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘爱华被灯塔市检察院批捕，后被起诉到灯塔市法院。刘爱华被关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">202</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被灯塔市法院第一次庭审，当日未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点，刘爱华被灯塔市法院第二次开庭后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/2/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432066.html#21101225216-1"><span style="color: windowtext;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/2/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432066.html#21101225216-1</span></a></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘伯滨</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年毕业于湖南大学，原为哈尔滨量具刃具厂（国有企业）高级工程师，由于坚持修炼使她受益的法轮大法，曾经被判刑五年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>至<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市、区三十多名法轮功学员被绑架，刘伯滨<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被香坊区警察抓捕、抄家、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日上午刘伯滨被哈尔滨市道里区法院视频远程开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金二万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘长富</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘长富并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对刘长富、李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。刘长富刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘春静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，因修炼法轮功，刘春静<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年曾被劳教两年，送佳木斯市西格木劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘春静在发放真相传单时，被人恶意构陷，又遭恶警抓捕被桦南县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押到黑龙江女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在街上递送给人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个护身符卡片，被举报，桦南县胜利派出所警察将刘春静抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘春静<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘春琴</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南省株洲市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原湖南省衡阳轧钢厂职工，一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘春琴多次被绑架、非法关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被株洲市天元区公安分局泰山路派出所恶警绑架；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被株洲市芦淞区法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被送湖南省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘翠梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘达鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林榆树市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。原籍吉林省舒兰市人，后搬到榆树市，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因信仰法轮功曾被劳教和判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刘达鹏与妻子李春环因在楼下自家车的车筐里发现别人放的真相资料，然后顺便发出去，被人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，榆树市正阳派出所五个警察闯入刘达鹏、李春环夫妇家中，将二人抓捕。刘达鹏被刑事拘留，妻子李春环被拘留五天。由于疫情，刘达鹏被取保候审一年，他们没被关在拘留所，而是被关押在正阳派出所，两天后，刘达鹏与妻子李春环被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，正阳派出所打电话让刘达鹏和李春环到派出所去一趟，刘达鹏被构陷到德惠市检察院，被批捕，并关押在榆树市看守所。后刘达鹏被德惠法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘德明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏南通维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日一早，无执法权的南通欣宏房屋征收服务有限公司受南通市港闸区住房和建设环境保护局委托，雇佣一批保安拥着挖掘机（犯罪工具），进入南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村，将刘德明的房屋团团围住，并拉上了警戒线，企图强拆，以达到非法圈地的目的。村民们向<span lang="EN-US">110</span>报警。港闸公安分局民警到达现场后，只是谈谈地说了一句：“政府行为，我们管不了”，致使非法圈地的保安更加有恃无恐，对刘德明家围困了整整一夜。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，该公司雇佣的保安用铁锤敲打刘德明的房屋。情势危急，且在民警不作为的情况下，刘德明为捍卫家园才点燃钩机。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南通市公安局港闸分局以涉嫌故意毁坏财产罪为由，将南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村村民刘德明带走调查。次日，该局作出港公（公）拘通字【<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>】<span lang="EN-US">263</span>号拘留通知书，载明对刘德明刑事拘留，现羁押于南通市看守所，并将拘留通知书向刘德明妻子送达。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘飞跃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">民生观察工作室负责人。湖北随州市人，自其<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年创办民生观察工作室以来，每逢敏感时期都会遭到来自随州当局以非法维稳为目的非法拘禁，和极不人道的殴打等形式的迫害、威胁，甚至殃及家属。刘飞跃先生<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日已被随州市公安局带走并刑事拘留，据消息称其罪名为涉嫌颠覆国家政权，起初其家属未得到书面通知。目前律师已经会见。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日刘飞跃先生涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案，在湖北随州市中院宣判，刘飞跃获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘富祥</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：重庆维权人士。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘富祥刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘广：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。男，职业医生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，警察闯入刘广有家诊所，将法轮功书籍掠走，并将刘广有抓捕关押、刑拘。后移交佳木斯市向阳区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日分别被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘广有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘海康：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江北安市法轮功学员。刘海康于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在家被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘海康的家人才得知刘海康已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现仍被关押在北安市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘汗：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士刘富祥的儿子。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘汗刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘洪兰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘洪兰、赵根法、黄春玲、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。刘洪兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘红枢</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：又名刘红书，陕西省岐山县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，岐山县京当镇祝家庄社区西戢村营西组人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，刘红枢修炼法轮大法。在法轮大法遭受迫害的最初那几年，刘红枢在新疆打工，在一家出版社工作，在讲法轮功被当地“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”人员绑架、失去了正常工作的机会，被非法劳教。此后经常受到岐山县、祝家庄乡政府人员的骚扰、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在家里被岐山县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>人员抓捕抄家，关押在岐山县看守所，后来被秘密开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5"><span style="color: windowtext;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘会茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，河北省人，知名民营企业家、河北大午农牧集团有限公司前董事长孙大午之妻，河北大午农牧有限公司核心创办人（之一），企业前高层管理者，挂职副监事长，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年起，因承包了一片荒弃的砖窑和坟包地作为投资养殖业，后历经几年发展，随促成与其丈夫孙大午共同创建河北大午农牧集团有限公司之行为，并成为丈夫创业、经营发展以及日后对社会“行公义，好怜悯”等作为的坚实后盾；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因河北大午农牧集团有限公司孙大午等<span lang="EN-US">25</span>位集团高管及亲属、亲信幕僚等被河北省高碑店市警方悉数带走，并被迅速以涉嫌“寻衅滋事、破坏生产经营罪”指定居所监视居住，其受牵连亦与两个儿媳等分别被带走、刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其年事已高，又患高血压、糖尿病等多种疾病，且早已不参与大午集团的决策和经营，既不涉及违法犯罪，也不涉及暴力性犯罪，其代理律师随为其先后两次申请变更强制措施（即取保候审），但两次均被警方以“经审查，我局认为刘会茹有可能毁灭、伪造证据、干扰证人作证“为由遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被高碑店市警方以涉嫌“非法吸收公众存款罪”转正式逮捕；后其案被高碑店市检察院起诉至至高碑店市法院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，终被河北省高碑店市法院一审以“非法吸收公众存款罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同案另两个儿媳及一个侄女被判定罪免罚。目前被羁押于河北省保定市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘家玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津静海县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年四十六岁。原静海县市容环卫局干部，静海县静海镇高庄子村人。她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年两次被非法关押在天津大港区板桥女子劳教所，前后五年遭受强制奴役劳动、不让睡觉等迫害，她坚持信仰，不妥协。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年才出狱。刘家玲<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，被关押在天津女子监狱，遭受残忍迫害。刘家玲在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又失踪，后得知被关押在静海看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获知刘家玲又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘建民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北邯郸市魏县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刘建民在广东省珠海市打工，在外面写“法轮大法好”标语，还百姓知情权。随后刘建民被珠海市斗门区国保大队抓捕到当地派出所拘留，后被批捕，并被起诉到珠海市斗门区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘建民被珠海市斗门区法院庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被非法关押在珠海市斗门区第二看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘建霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省三门峡人，五十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七二零后，因去北京为法轮大法鸣冤而遭抓捕，后被非法劳教，劫持到郑州十八里河劳教所，后来又被三门峡法院判刑六年。她曾被迫流离失所多年。三门峡“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>” 到处查找她，在全国非法通缉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘建霞与法轮功学员杨中省被跟踪抓捕。刘建霞曾在河南省新乡女子监狱被关小号折磨<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多天，被迫害得脸肿、胸闷等“哮喘”症状已经一年多，现在越来越重，生命垂危，据悉每天靠大量药物维持生存。当年与刘建霞一起被抓捕的法轮功学员杨中省，被非法关押没有几天，就于二零一六年四月在郑州第三看守所被迫害致死。刘建霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">福建福州维权人士。福州市仓山区城门镇前锦村村民。刘建新因房屋被强拆近<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，至今无补偿、无安置<span lang="EN-US">.</span>在去年，刘建新因在家被<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时监控，感到非常郁闷，去北京旅游散心，结果遭到维稳人员劫持后被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。因为刘建新在北京既没有信访，更没有违法行为，最后公安只能将其放了。后来，当时的城门镇赵书记就刘建新的诉求组织了一次协调，因为政府不愿意就其违法强拆行为，依法给予安置与赔偿，双方协商未能成功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘建新在北京永定门河边举“冤”字牌，然后跳下去准备了此被官府肆意欺压与压迫的屈辱一生，然后被保安救上来。到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号晩上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，刘建新被送到城门派岀所，关在城门派岀所铁笼里面，其妻子得知消息后赶到，一直等到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号晚上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点之后，派出所告知刘建新被送走了。后获悉其被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被正式批捕。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘杰（山东）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东枣庄市薛城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘杰和魏延景出去张贴法轮功宣传不干胶被永福派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，山东枣庄市薛城区法院开庭宣判，判决刘杰<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金三万元，魏延景<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并罚金五千元。刘杰当庭宣布上诉。刘杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘杰（黑龙江）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江哈尔滨市宾县维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的刘杰，是因为在<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年做生意时，经销的<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余万商品被检察院扣押拒不返回、且销毁案件的案卷材料而上访。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刘杰在北京时，哈尔滨市宾县政府的领导多次给刘杰打电话，说别去国家信访局登记了，回来就给解决问题，还给刘杰买了机票回宾县。当刘杰回宾县后，政法委书记刘宇峰确实组织了听证会，但提出给予<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万困难补助，一次性解决刘杰的诉求，刘杰拒绝了这样的解决方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘杰因对由政法委书记刘宇峰组织的听证结果表达不满，被宾县公安局以辱骂了政法委书记刘宇峰为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年“七一”建党百年前夕，宾县公安局曾以刘杰在今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日到检察院辱骂工作人员为由，又以“寻衅滋事”为由对刘杰拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天。今年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘杰再次去北京上访，在北京拦截了国家信访局大局长李文章的车，被宾县公安局以“寻衅滋事”为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。后刘杰的女儿接到辖区派出所电话，告知其父亲已经被刑事拘留，送看守所羁押。刘杰的女儿问自己父亲已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁了，之前已两次被行政拘留，是否符合合并为刑事拘留的规定？派出所没有给予回答。据了解，刘杰患有严重高血压、高血压脂、心脏病，且是<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁的老人了，已不符合羁押式拘留的规定，现在宾县公安又升级为刑事拘留，看来一心想要维护合法权益的刘老汉是凶多吉少了。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，刘又杰被被举报单位宾县检察院正式批捕。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体;
