font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁沈阳的维权人士。刘丽是为父亲刘树义劳工权益而上访了十一年。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，时年已经<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的刘树义为了活命，还在沈阳市苏家屯八一镇政府内烧锅炉，为里面“全心全意为人民服务”的官员做苦力。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">19</span>点，加班的刘树义在上班途中遭遇车祸，按照劳动合同法的规定，用人单位应该以工伤予以补偿，但八一镇政府因为没有为劳动者办理工伤保险，就拒绝承担工伤责任，作为女儿的刘丽开始替父上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘丽到了北京府右街后被截访送马家楼，然而有沈阳市苏家屯区的截访人员接回。后遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刘丽因“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被检察院批捕。暂无案件后续信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">刘敏杰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：河北省保定市定州市人，人称“维权能手”，人权捍卫者。曾因儿子刘强从部队退伍后做生意被抢劫杀害，而最高法院未公开审理就直接改判，以致主凶未受到应有的惩罚，随认为此举属于认定事实错误、违反法定程序，从而进京上访维权十余年，其间，其申诉冤案不仅没得到纠正，反被属地和北京等司法机关以莫须有的罪名劳教、拘留多次，还被接访官员打断几根肋骨，且因多次被毒打，患上神经性脊髓炎，眼睛也几近失明。近年来，因其在北京最高检、最高法、国家信访局，全国人大信访接待处及中央领导、巡视组寄信继续揭露最高法院的办案黑幕，虽引起中纪委等领导重视，但却遭到最高法院等司法部门的打击报复，曾被最高法院法警多次殴打、关小黑屋虐待，被地方公检法以各种方式截访等。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日其被最高法院法警和北京东交民巷派出所警方突然联合抓捕，次日被移交至河北省定州市警方，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-23</span>日先后被以涉“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被河北省定州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服，已当庭提起上诉。目前被关押在河北省定州市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘明萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘明萍被宁波江北区庄桥派出所警察抓捕抄家。后获悉刘明萍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到浙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。刘平被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、非法占用农用地罪、寻衅滋事罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">28</span>日被特警在其租住房内抓捕。当天，大连政法委策划，采用手机监控、跟踪、定位、蹲坑等手段，在大连地区各县区同一时间统一行动，抓捕了数十名法轮功学员，有很多人当天被放回，有的当月回家，最后还有多人被判刑。这次抓捕被公安国保称为“<span lang="EN-US">1614</span>”大案。刘仁秋、盛杰、谷树春、王红玉四名法轮功学员，被旅顺法院二次非法开完庭后，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下判决书， 刘仁秋被判<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘伟<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都市法轮功学员。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被成都公安局成华分局国保、双水碾派出所警察抄家并抓捕。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被成华区公安分局批捕，关押在郫县看守所。构陷他们的所谓「案件」曾两次退回侦查机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，成华区检察院把刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇起诉到成华区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇，在成都市成华区法院一楼视频开庭，分别被判刑八年。庭审结束后，夫妻俩与家人坚决不服判决，马上要求上诉，并请律师继续代理二审。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘卫国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，北京市丰台区人，化名刘于谦，北京源佳科技公司职员，自由信仰者，新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市常驻居民，“耶和华见证人”教派信徒，前重庆会众长老，前新疆伊犁会众长老，库尔勒会众长老，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，自从在北京基督某教派“耶和华见证人”受洗以来，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被派往重庆举行传教，后被安立（任命）为重庆会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又前往新疆伊犁市做伊犁会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又被任命库尔勒会众长老；因曾大力发展教会信徒，举办会众参加圣经培训及举办<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多次家庭聚会，从而引起库尔勒市当局关注；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因曾两次参加“耶和华见证人”香港分部的区域大会，后又在库尔勒楼兰世家组织聚会，随被库尔勒市民宗委查处；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，因曾到韩国参加过区域大会，遂再遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，与多人被巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市警方悉数抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪 ”转正式被捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人被库尔勒市检察院提起公诉，指控其所属教会与正统基督教教义不符，宣传“政治中性”，要求信徒“不履行国家宪法，不参加爱国主义教育，不服兵役，不入党，不如团，不升国旗，不唱国歌，不向国旗敬礼”等，同时又打着基督教旗号，积极发展组织成员，多次组织、提供场所进行聚会，故而触犯了政府法律规定，属于参与邪教的违法行为；截至目前，其具体信息缺详，至今未审待判。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">刘湘菊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省沈阳市辽中区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘湘菊在向村民发放法轮功真相台历时，被辽中区公安局警察绑架。第二天，辽中区城郊派出所警察去她家抄家，在她家无人的情况下，私自掠走了她丈夫打工挣来的九千元现金。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刘湘菊女士被辽中区法院非法庭审，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下达判决书，被非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘晓慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省济南市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，家住济南天桥区黄屯小区六区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早上七点多，在家中被天桥区公安国保大队和无影山派出所警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留，被关押到济南看守所。刘晓慧被关押一年六个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被济南市天桥区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘兴国</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省潢川县白店乡白店村的农民，生于<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年，今年已经整整<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，国家<span lang="EN-US">1704</span>粮食储备库建到了白店乡白店村，根据刘兴国获取的该粮食储备库的审计表显示，给予集体经济组织的补偿总共才<span lang="EN-US">350</span>余万人民币（失地农民并没有足额拿到这些补偿），却给白店乡政府征地的奖励达<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万人民币，加上给参与征地的派出所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万、媒体<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万元人民币。更令刘兴国感到不安的，是该<span lang="EN-US">1704</span>国家粮食储备库自从建成后，居然没有储存<span lang="EN-US">1</span>斤可食用的粮食，而是收进只能用于工业的陈化粮以套取国家补助而中饱私囊。当年“三面红旗”时期差一点被饿死的刘兴国，就同村民徐耀辉、王国强、王金国、蔡金芳、陈德琴、郑庆梅等，向国家机关及国内媒体投诉举报，还持证据材料到北京有关部门信访反映。正因为刘兴国的进京信访行为，遭来了地方官吏的疯狂打压，在刘兴国遭到暴力截访后，多次被处以治安拘留，还在白店乡派出所对其实施酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年年全国“两会”期间，刘兴国在北京再次遭到潢川县公安局驻京的刘桂红等人的截访，到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日（农历<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初二）被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，到<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘学荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省烟台市牟平区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。刘学荣老人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午在牟平区集贸市场发法轮大法资料，被便衣警察绑架，随后被关押到烟台市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，牟平区公检法机构秘密对老人判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，家住武穴市城区，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刘艳峰刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳华<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南周口市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被中共劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，之后多次被骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，刘艳华及丈夫刘冲还有到她家串门的法轮功学员杜子良，被河南省周口市公安局荷花分局四、五个警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年元月，刘艳华被河南周口市川汇区法院第三刑事庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，家属毫不知情。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生于<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年，湖北荆门公民，人权捍卫者。原是荆门市一间银行的职员。刘艳丽是因网上公布与国保的对话记录，因言获罪<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日遭刑事拘留，罪名竟然是“诽谤罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日又被逮捕。共被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日取保获释。刘艳丽主要做帮助抗战老兵工作，是一名追求民主自由人士，网上言论较多，是一位政治异见人士。刘艳丽<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午开始被荆门公安国保传唤。后获知刘艳丽遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘艳丽女士因言获罪，被荆门市东宝区法院以寻衅滋事罪判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东河源市知名维权律师。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生。刘尧是自学成为律师，曾专门受理农民与开发商及地方官员间的“征地”纠纷案件。刘尧第一次出名是在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2007</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，当时他因参与一场农村抗议活动被拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2008</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，刘尧被判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。此前，刘尧所代表的村民与一个水电站的保安人员对峙，检方称，有价值</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币的建筑材料在对峙中被毁坏。对这个情节较轻的案件，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年的结果在中国法律界引起抗议。法律人士纷纷为他辩护。当时是李方平和浦志强等维权律师代理他进行了一系列上诉，最终使刘尧的刑期减为</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月监禁。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月下旬，刘尧实名向中共广东省纪检委举报，并在网上发文，指河源市委书记何忠友非法支持广东康泉十八国际生态健康旅游城有限公司违法占用农地，包括基本农田的项目，修建高尔夫球场。中国的法规（基本农田保护条例第</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">条）明确规定任何单位和个人不得改变或者占用基本农田。同时，刘尧还向纪检委举报当时河源市公安局局长彭定邦毫无理由地停止调查</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名商人销售假冒著名韶关钢铁公司品牌的钢材，敦促纪委以涉嫌受贿的问题调查彭定邦。没多久，于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被河源市公安局源城分局以涉嫌“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”（后撤销指控）和“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被广东河源市源城区法院以“敲诈勒索罪”、“诈骗罪”和“收买被拐卖的儿童罪”数罪并罚，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑，罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">140</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">221,000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">美元）。刘尧认为，他被起诉和定罪，是因为他长期举报河源市党政官员的贪腐行为，而遭到河源市</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多名纪检、检察、法院官员“帮助腐败党政高官报复陷害”。后上诉、申诉均遭驳回。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2036</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">刘义波<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刘义波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘银凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁凤城市红旗镇法轮功学员。<a name="_Hlk52322012">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。</a>刘银凤<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日去黄旗赶集买鸡蛋，回家途中被红旗派出所抓捕抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被凤城法院庭审，后获悉刘银凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺市清原县<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的法轮功学员，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在贴“法轮大法好”粘贴时被警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日遭清原县法院庭审，后被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年的一天，经人介绍刘玉开始学炼法轮功。刘玉曾患有胃癌，因修炼法轮功才得以康复。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，刘玉用自己的亲身经历向民众讲述大法的美好，揭穿中共喉舌媒体谎言。为此刘玉多次遭绑架、关押：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年冬天被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日再次被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被绑架，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；回家不到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘玉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日再次被绑架，后又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁铁岭市法轮功学员。刘玉华和丈夫靳利国都修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，刘玉华和靳利国曾遭中共多次绑架、关押。由于此前靳利国和刘玉华夫妇往一些公检法部门邮寄了“明真相 保平安”的劝善信，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，铁岭市昌图县国保大队封锁了靳利国和刘玉华夫妇家的楼道，谎称抓“杀人犯”，闯入靳利国和刘玉华夫妇家里，实施抓捕和抄家， 后刘玉华被铁岭市昌图县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；丈夫靳利国被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，身体十分虚弱的刘玉华被转入辽宁省女子监狱迫害。据悉，在看守所非法关押期间，刘玉华被迫害得很严重，导致血压高达<span lang="EN-US">200mmHg</span>，糖代谢紊乱，血糖高达<span lang="EN-US">14mmol</span>／<span lang="EN-US">L</span>（空腹血糖正常值：<span lang="EN-US">3.9</span>～<span lang="EN-US">5.5mmol</span>／<span lang="EN-US">L</span>），骨瘦如柴。而且，刘玉华左臂麻木，左腿动不了，检查结果是腔隙性脑梗。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">刘玉秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省鹤岗市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日刘玉秋在家被当地警察断电抓捕，关押在鹤岗市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月得知刘玉秋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，已被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">刘玉霞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：女，现年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，河南省平顶山市人，原在市政府物价局工作，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功遭迫害，曾被多次送“洗脑班”、拘留，甚至被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并在新乡女子监狱服刑，遭非人虐待，同时被单位开除，无任何生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午七点多，刘玉霞在路上发邀请函，请人们旁听法轮功信仰者穆亚东的庭审，结果又被光明路派出所抓捕，后关押到平顶山宝丰县看守所。由于刘玉霞不报姓名，直到下午七点，派出所根据手纹用技术手段才查出刘玉霞的身份和住址。晚上八点，其家被查抄，搜走法轮功书籍多本、未发出去的邀请函及几个真相光盘等。随后，她就被刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘玉霞被平顶山市新华区法院一审重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。其不服上诉，后经平顶山市中级法院不公开审理，依然维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日她已被送往到河南省新乡女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘增奎</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>至<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市、区三十多名法轮功学员被绑架，刘增奎于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被香坊区警察抓捕、抄家、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日上午刘增奎被哈尔滨市道里区法院视频远程开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘珍俐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市东西湖区女法轮功学员。原武汉东西湖新沟镇棉纺织厂职工。仅仅因为法轮功学员的身份，刘珍俐曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕、关押在洗脑班；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，她被抓捕到何湾劳教所劳教；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日刘珍俐在自家门口被东西湖区吴家山街派出所抓捕、关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，获悉其于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘志峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘志峰等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，刘志峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柳德玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆门市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，曾多次遭到迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月历经<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年残酷迫害后，从范家台监狱黑窝回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在讲法轮功时又被绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，荆门市东宝区法院庭审柳德玉，历时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分钟。当场未宣布刑期。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，柳德玉被冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被转到湖北沙洋范家台监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳木兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市新洲区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，武汉新洲区农家妇女，曾遭中共冤狱迫害三年半，被迫害致非常消瘦、精神恍惚。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中午，在租住地，被便衣警察绑架，后一直被关押在武汉市第一看守所，看守所将不明药物偷偷放在她的饭里面。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月下旬才得知，柳木兰被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索四千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柳秋生：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西省九江市法轮功学员，都昌县人。柳秋生原来在都昌县调查队从事统计调查工作（公务员）。因为坚持信仰真善忍，遭迫害被开除公职，没有生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，柳秋生遭抓捕。非法抄家时抄收现金六万元还有存款和五万美元存单。构陷编造的罪名是“里通外国”，其实是柳秋生家中房屋拆迁款，柳秋生在银行的同学帮助存了美元存单，取不了，美元只是利息高点，这笔钱是留给儿子读大学用的。当局给柳秋生强按的罪名是“里通外国”，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被九江市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳全春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，辽宁省大石桥市旗口镇农民，法轮功学员。辽宁大石桥市法轮功学员柳全春、史庆秀夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭营口市站前区法院在看守所庭审，两位律师出庭为他们进行无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，法官赵丹就下了判决：分别判刑柳全春和史庆秀<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，并没收所有扣押的物品。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省绵阳市法轮功学员。柳涛女士，大学毕业后在深圳工作。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七月江泽民迫害法轮功后，她讲法轮功真相，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在广东三水劳教所因炼功被每个犯人各抽<span lang="EN-US">30</span>鞭子等残暴迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日在绵阳市再次被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，在四川女子监狱遭吊在钢管上毒打，被强制戴手铐脚镣、关小号、不准睡觉等酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，绵阳市法轮功学员柳涛与三台县法轮功学员邓成开到三台县芦溪镇去买东西被抓捕。柳涛被关押在绵阳市看守所，邓成开被关押在三台县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，柳涛、邓承开被绵阳市三台县法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金二千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢凤花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">青岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十五岁，家住青岛市西海岸新区胶南办事处象沟头村。在中共迫害法轮功持续至今近二十年中，卢凤花曾被判刑八年，在济南监狱被迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在家包粽子，被胶南派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被胶南检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢桂芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北涞水县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1940</span>年代生人，家住涞水县王村乡辛庄头村的农家妇女。在中共对法轮功持续至今与二十一年的迫害中，屡遭中共迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日再次被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前卢桂芬老人仍被非法关押在保定看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢永良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南岳阳市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，卢永良在家中与几位法轮功学员一起读法轮大法著作。被警察入户抓捕，并抄家。电脑、打印机、刻录机、大法书籍、真相资料等私人物品被警察抄走。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。卢永良被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被湖南省平江县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，没收电脑、打印机、刻录机、装订机等。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢志英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：卢志英被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陆建华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，上海市人，前中国最高层核心智囊之一，第二届“北京市十大杰出青年”，曾任中国社会科学院社会学研究所研究员、公共政策研究中心副主任，中央电视台特约评论员和重庆市渝北区副区长等职，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，因陆续为香港记者程翔提供<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余篇稿件，其中<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月所提供的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>篇文章内容被中共视为涉及“国家绝密资料”，遂于<span lang="EN-US"> 2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被国家安全局秘密拘捕；后经秘密审判，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市第二中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 20</span>年；其上诉坚称自己被冤，均被驳回。目前在北京市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆建荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏讨薪农民工、维权公民。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年先后两次于六四敏感日因转发中国公民及国际友人在驻美中国大使馆门口举行纪念“六<span lang="EN-US">.</span>四”活动的图片遭到警方传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被江苏警方跨省抓捕，涉嫌“非法买卖枪支弹药罪”，至今不被释放，被刑拘于泰兴市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">鲁•贡确嘉措：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海省黄南州尖扎县拉莫德钦寺僧人，因写书记录流亡印度觐见达赖喇嘛尊者的经历，近日第二次遭当局带走，目前与外界失联。鲁•贡确嘉措将自己翻越雪山、赴印拜见达赖喇嘛尊者的过程，写成名为《五十四天》的书籍。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年年底完稿后被警方约谈，带到黄南州国安局非法扣留审问长达一周之久，并被警告不得出版该书。获释后不满一个月，贡确嘉措再次被当局约谈，目前与外界失联。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，黄南州统战部打电话约谈，他回复说等雪停了后再去，结果下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分左右，两名黄南州安全局的人员将他带走，之后便没有了任何消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲁孟君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（鲁梦军、鲁梦君）女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，湖南省湘潭市法轮功学员。家住湖南省湘潭市护潭乡繁城村向荣组，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年下半年走上修炼法轮功之路。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，鲁孟君曾两次被判刑，每次判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，共<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年冤狱，在湖南省女子监狱遭受酷刑体罚折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，鲁孟君被湘潭市雨湖区公安分局警察抓捕、抄家，关押在湘潭市看守所，不准家人见面，在家人不知任何情况之下，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日第三次被劫入湖南省女子监狱。据悉鲁孟君被判刑七年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鲁扬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，本名张桂祺，网名“鲁西狂徒”，山东省莘县人，著名诗人。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年开始诗歌文学创作活动，创办“扬子宛诗社”，并主编出版《扬子宛诗刊》。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年创办“中国当代诗歌论坛”，出版主编《中国当代诗歌》刊物。二年后“中国当代诗论坛”被封。期间开始在《星星》、《诗选刊》等国内著名诗歌刊物上发表诗歌。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年创办“中国自由文化论坛”，因颇有影响而被迫多次关停，后移入外网“自由中国”网站，最后又移入博讯网站。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因自由写作被迫于聊城外国学校辞职，后妻子工作也受到牵连，一起离开山东，南方谋生，此间由诗歌创作转入文化自由写作，大量作品发表于国内各大网站，并被海外多家网站转载。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与“零八宪章”签署，夫妻工作再次受到影响，双双失业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，为支持入狱的本会前会长刘晓波而入独立中文笔会。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年受“茉莉花运动”影响，再次失业并遭遣返回山东老家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因举牌声援批评毛泽东遭解职的山东广播电视台特约评论员邓相超教授，在邓教授所在的济南建筑大学遭到暴徒殴打，受到中外媒体关注，同时也成为有关部门重点监控对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年创办“中国诗人大讲堂——文殊书院”，继续从事自由文化传播事业。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方带走，下落不明近两个星期，后被聊城市公安局以“涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪”宣布刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日已被秘密开庭，家属竟然被封锁，对此一无所知。关押于聊城市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">栾凝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，大学文化，原来在宁夏劳动人事厅工作，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功前，是宁夏法轮功辅导站副站长（义务教功）。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，栾凝到兴庆区一邮政储蓄所邮寄信件。栾凝离开后，被该所人员以信件涉及法轮功内容向派出所报警，并将信件交给派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，栾凝上班时在家门口被抓捕。宁夏银川市中级法院在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下达判决书，对栾凝判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛迪嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区索县若达乡索卡村人，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Lodoe Gyamtso</span>，西藏民间舞蹈艺术家，藏族人权捍卫者，异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初，曾因其姐、妹二人在一场车祸中被司机撞死及遭到谋杀，而当时的那曲地方法院竟枉法以该司机为亲共藏人为由，判其“无罪”；同年晚些时候，两人在村庄市场相遇，随发生争执冲突，冲突中为了躲避司机方对其的两次射杀，其被迫自卫，刺伤了司机，致使该司机虽送医院仍最终死亡；针此，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被西藏那曲中级法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后送拉萨市扎奇监狱服刑；服刑期间，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又曾因在扎奇监狱带领狱友高喊“西藏独立”，“中国退出西藏”，“祈愿达赖喇嘛尊者长久住世”，“六百万藏人要团结”等口号进行抗议，并散发手写传单<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多份，在遭受审讯及酷刑折磨<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月之后，被西藏当局决定处于死刑，后在联合国及国际特赦等组织的干预下，才未对其施行处决，但又加刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被转至拉萨市曲水监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其终获刑满获释，但又被软禁在家<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因公开谴责中共西藏当局强迫居住在西藏巴青县、索县和比如县的藏人中共八一建军节时穿珍贵野兽皮毛饰品（此为传统藏人服饰，但藏人已从<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年始自愿放弃穿戴该饰品）和表演歌舞等，并将其认同的达赖喇嘛提出的解决西藏问题的“中间道路”和“和平区”等概念，以及对佛教姻缘和非暴力原则重要性的感悟和认识，让其妻噶吉拍录视频，广为传播，而遭致当局的仇视与严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又曾因公开反对中共当局强令除在西藏之外，在藏区其他各地寺院里学习的僧侣、尼师必须限期返回索县和比如县等，否则其家属将面临遭监禁和接受禁止挖虫草处罚等非人道作法（挖虫草是当地藏人经济收入的最主要来源），随再遭当局拘押，并关押在比如县监狱中，后因健康状况不佳，才准予释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因在拉萨市布达拉宫前举行抗议活动，并在网上发视频，宣称自己正在发起一场“世界和平运动”，引起海外流亡藏人广泛热议，随被那曲地区索县警方再次拘捕，并被以“国家机密案”论处；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被西藏自治区那曲县中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”再次重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前在拉萨市扎什监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛米（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，本名嘉央，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡三村人，阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学员，非暴力追求者，藏族知名作家，中国在押良心犯。因长期在藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学习，且爱撰写发表、出版许多相关文章及书籍（如《弥漫的橙黄烟雾》等），从而成为海内外藏人区域知名的僧人作家，又因平素崇尚非暴力，致力于藏母语保护宣传，深受藏人及境内外网友喜爱；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被阿坝县警方突然秘密抓捕，罪由不清，自此失联；其家人、亲友及寺庙僧侣等均感震惊、担忧，其同为作家的友人疑称可能与其发表、撰写了关乎西藏命运的文章，尤其从事了环保活动有关；后知其被当局转正式逮捕，并关押于汶川县看守所；羁押期间，其饱受酷刑折磨，并在庭审前曾被利诱，要求为官方做事，称其若答应则可为其家人提供经济援助，并准其出境旅游等，若不答应则将重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，但被其断然拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案被阿坝藏族羌族自治州法院秘密庭审，最终在未通知家属旁听的情况下被以“颠覆国家政权罪”、“泄漏国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前在四川省汶川监狱（德阳市黄许镇阿坝监狱或绵阳市川北监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑慈诚（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族良心犯。洛桑慈诚和洛桑祥曲两名年轻僧人于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被当地警方从格尔登寺院抓走后，长达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月一直没有任何消息。他们被当局指控涉嫌与自焚僧人扎白事件有关。洛桑慈诚，是阿坝县求吉玛乡人，当年<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬被当局秘密（没有通知家属情况下）判处<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">洛桑次仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县格德寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在阿坝县城街道上，手持一幅达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，呼喊着“嘉瓦丹增嘉措万岁”疾步行走，独自游街表达了对达赖喇嘛尊者的虔诚信仰，随后被中共公安人员控制带走。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑丹增（藏<span lang="EN-US">/</span>左贡寺高僧）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年左右出生，西藏自治区昌都市左贡县旺达镇乌雅村人，又称乌雅•朱古（即转世喇嘛）洛桑丹增仁波切，早年曾在阿里地区任职导游和司机，后成为西藏左贡寺高僧。曾因经常到西藏的左贡县左贡寺劝导僧俗民众停止供奉所谓的“朵杰凶天”，而要为西藏民族的长远理想和第十四世达赖喇嘛的健康长寿着想，并鼓励藏人努力保护、发扬民族宗教与文化等，受到藏人僧俗的广泛爱戴和尊敬，随招致中共当局的恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在西藏拉萨市被左贡县警方抓走刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，被西藏自治区左贡县法院以“追随达赖分裂集团”、“劝诫、蛊惑地方藏民停止修供凶天”等为罪由，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑格培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡第二大队人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，曾因政治诉求于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被当局抓捕并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被提前数月释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，其直到一个月前仍处于下落不明状态，且当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑嘉扬（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝自治州阿坝县僧人，现年<span lang="EN-US">28</span>岁，笔名为“鲁米”的藏人作家，是阿坝县麦尔玛乡第三村人。嘉杨自小在阿坝格德寺出家为僧，几年前遭中共当局从该寺驱逐后，前往色达喇荣五明佛学院等佛教寺院继续修学佛法。因在著作中自由表达观点便于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人获悉他在两个月前被中共当局指控“泄露国家机密”与“分裂国家”罪非法判处了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半有期徒刑。洛桑嘉杨告诉前去探视的亲属，他从未做过触犯法律的事情，也从未向当局“承认”过什么罪行。现在汶川县某监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑克珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">44</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因政治诉求被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后因当时在狱中受虐严重，导致罹患重病而被提前释放，后经由家人、亲友自筹经费，让其住院长时治疗，才得以转危为安。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其因被指控涉嫌“在微信建立组群为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿，特别收集长寿祈愿文持诵及持咒数量”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑曲达（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">西藏安多阿坝县格德寺僧人。中共当局最初在阿坝等地开展“爱国爱教”运动时，他就曾表达不满，并在县政府前张贴文字进行抗议，当时被判处了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年徒刑。出狱后于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与当地的和平抗议活动，呼喊出达赖喇嘛返回西藏的诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被中共警方再次抓捕，约一年后被阿坝县中级人民法院指控“煽动分裂国家”、“代领民众开展示威”，遭判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，现在四川省绵阳监狱中服刑，近日获悉其身体健康状况出现严重问题。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑桑杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，青海省果洛州久治县人，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺（又译格德寺）僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因向外透露格尔登寺僧人自焚抗议事件真相，而被中共当地警方抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并被追加指控涉嫌制作、出售达赖喇嘛的相片和讲法的影片等，违法了中国法律，遂于当年被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日秘密获释；据悉，其在狱中因遭受酷刑虐待，以致出狱时身体状况极差，出现丧失记忆症状；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其再次被当地警方以涉嫌藏人自焚抗议等“政治问题”抓捕、刑拘；在非法关押长达<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月之后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院一审以“政治问题”（不知名罪名）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日；因当地对藏族群体高压严控情况十分严重，故其具体情况缺详。目前其羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛桑坦凯（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿坝县格尔登寺僧人。他<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁。他自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，也是曾被中国当局关闭的寺属学校“佛学青年文苑”第三届毕业生，被捕前在格尔登寺辩经学院中观班就读。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被捕，具体日期不详。洛桑坦凯于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。除此之外，有关他被指控的罪名、被关押的地点等情况，因为当局过度的言行限制及网络审查而无法进一步了解。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县安斗乡克洼村人，当地知名画家东阔之子，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因政治诉求而被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被警方带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗保军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗昌平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日生，湖南涟源人。现为天椒法务集团董事长，中欧国际工商学院<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>级<span lang="EN-US">EMBA</span>学员，历任《新京报》核心报道记者、深度报道部主编，《财经》杂志副主编兼任《<span lang="EN-US">LENS</span>视觉》杂志副主编。著有《递罪》、《打铁记》、《高官反腐录》。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，罗昌平因在新浪微博就长津湖战役发表“半个世纪之后国人少有反思这场战争的正义性，就像当年的沙雕连不会怀疑上峰的『英明决策』。”之言论，被中国内地官媒谴责。同日《解放军报》旗下媒体「钧正平」、共青团中央官方微博等官媒发文认为罗昌平在恶意诋毁英烈，随后其新浪微博账户被封禁。后罗昌平于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日就三亚警方带走调查。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日海南公安的新浪微博官方账号通报，三亚市吉安公安局以涉嫌「侮辱英烈」的「违法言论」，对其刑事拘留，同时表示「英雄烈士不容亵渎」，指公安机关会严厉查处网络上不同方式有害英烈名誉、荣誉的行为。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，罗昌平因言获罪被以涉嫌侵害英雄烈士名誉、荣誉罪，海南省三亚市城郊检察院以涉嫌侵害英雄烈士名誉、荣誉罪对罗昌平批准逮捕。对罗昌平的批捕是中共当局肆无忌惮镇压不同言论，践踏公民言论自由权利的又一例证。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/v_22.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/v_22.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">抚顺市望花区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁的罗纯贵老人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在古城子第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>中学附近讲真相，被警察抓捕，由于疫情，回家被监视居住。古城子派出所警察经常到他家骚扰，后来望花检察院也去骚扰，对罗纯贵起诉，罗纯贵被迫流离失所。警察还经常到家找他儿子骚扰，他儿子不配合，拒绝回答。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，罗纯贵去建设市场时被电子眼拍到，被抓捕到建设派出所，后被望花法院秘密开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。现被关押抚顺看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/9/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%BD%97%E7%BA%AF%E8%B4%B5%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430595.html"><span
